 The operator will send a verification code to the customer's number for re-verification through the Aadhaar card

 " aadesh main yah bhi kaha gaya he ki ek i-kevysi par ek se zyada mobile conection kaa veriphication kiya ja saktaa he lekin kai numberon kaa nahin

 doorsanchaar vibhaag ne sabhi doorsanchaar companiyon ko notice jari karke kaha he ki desh main maujuud sabhi mobile numberon ko kevysi process ke jariye dobaaraa se satyaapan karavaaya jaae
 Aadhaar card will also be added to KYC (know Your Customer)
 vibhaag ne nirdesh die hai ki yadi kisi number kaa satyaapan nahin hota he yaa phir aadhaar number se nahin joda jaataa he to vah number band ho jayega

 " The order also states that more than one mobile connection can be verified on one e-kyc but not many numbers

 rishte main sunil gavaskar ke bahanoi vishwanath ne england ke wicketiper ballebaaj bob tailor ko ampire dwaara out qaraar die jane ke baad bhi ballebaaji ke liye bulaayaa tha
 Vishwanath was the captain of the Indian team in this match
 haalanki tailor ko ballebaaji ke liye waapas bulaane kaa faisla bhartiya team ko baari padaa tha or use yah test 10 wicket se ganvaana padaa tha, lekin cricket jagat main 'vishi' ke is faisle ko mile kaa pathar mana jaataa he or ise us samay bharpoor saraahna mili thi
 At that time, many newspapers had given a headline referring to this incident, 'shabas Vishwanath
 
 
 
 Comments yah ghatana farvari 1980 main bharat or england ke bich khele gaye test match kii he
 The Indian team was dismissed for just 242 runs in the first innings, batting first in this Golden Jubilee Test played at the Wankhede Stadium in Mumbai (then Bombay)
 jawaab main bhartiya tej gendbaajon kii tikdi, kapildev, karsan ghavri or roger binni ne england kii bhi shuruyaat bigaad di thi
 At one time five batsmen from England were dismissed for 58 runs
 is samay harfanmaulaa ian botham or wicketiper ballebaaj bob tailor saajhedaari kar england team ko sanvaarane kii koshish main jute tailor jab 43 ranon par khel rahe the tabhi kapil dev kii gendbaaji par bhartiya team ne wicket ke peeche kaich kii apil kii or ampire ne unhen out qaraar de diya
 Despite the umpire's decision, Bob Taylor did not consider himself out and stood at the crease
 vishwanath is halaat ko dekhakar, tailor ke paas gaye or unase poocha ki kya aapke balle kaa kinaaraa laga he, tailor ne inkaar kar diya tab vishi ne ampire ke paas jaakar faisla badalane kii apil kii
 On this great initiative of Vishwanath, Bob Taylor again got a chance to bat
 vaise, yah alag baat he ki botham-tailor kii jodi ne chathe wicket ke liye 171 ran kii saajhedaari kar match kii tasviir badal di
 Botham scored 114 and Taylor scored 43 runs in this match
 england kii pehali pari 296 ran par samaapt hui or use 54 ran kii badhat mili
 In the second innings, the Indian team was piled on for just 149 runs in front of England fast bowler Ian Botham (seven wickets for 48 runs)
 match main england ko jeet ke liye 96 ran kaa target mila tha jo usne bina koi wicket khoe hasil kar liya tha
 Of course, this test match was won by the England team by 10 wickets, but the winner of the match was Indian captain Vishwanath as he won the hearts of sports lovers by presenting the best example of sportsmanship

 kallis ne gendbaaji main bhi jalawaa dikhaate hue chaar over main 21 ran dekar do wicket chatkaaye

 isse pehle suresh raina (44) or captain mahendra singh dhoni (naabad 34) kii pariyon ke baavjood chennai superkings kii team paanch wicket par 139 ran hi bana saki

 unhone braavo kii gend par ek ran ke saath 43 gend main ardhashatak puraa kiya or phir isi over main lagaataar do chauke bhi jade
 Morkel, however, caught Tiwari in the hands of Yo Mahesh

 Earlier, Chennai started off to bat after winning the toss and lost the openers of both openers Faf du Plessis (03) and Mike Hussey (18) by 32 runs in five overs
 plasis ne pari ke duusare over main tej gendbaaj brett lee kii gend par wicketiper brandan maikulam ko kaich thamaya jabaki austrailia kaa westeindies daura samaapt hone ke baad team se jude hasi ran lene kii jaldbaaji main pavilion laute
 Bravo was lucky on a personal score of 11 when his West Indies off-spinner Naren bowled a wide ball on the leg side to see him go ahead but mccullum missed a stump chance
 braavo haalanki is jeevandaan kaa phayda nahin uthaa sake or kallis kii gend ko uthaakar maarane kii koshish main long aan par abdulla ko kaich de baithe
 The comments kolkata ke gendbaajon ne is bich chennai ke ballebaajon par shikanja kasnaa shuru kiya or 46 gend tak koi chaukaa yaa chakka nahin laga
 Under pressure to increase the run pace, Raina flew into the air trying to send Kallis's ball for six runs and Yusuf Pathan took an easy catch while running from midwicket
 unhone 34 gend main chaar chauke or ek chakka jadaa
 Dhoni and Ravindra Jadeja also failed to increase the run pace
 dhoni ne 17wein over main lee par chauke ke saath boundry ke sookhe ko khatm kiya

 3 over main 100 ran ke aankade ko chuaa
 Jadeja once again failed and became the victim of Naren after scoring nine runs off 13 balls
 albi morkal 13 ran banaakar naabad rahe

 gambhir ne 52 gend main chah chaukon or ek chakke kii madad se 63 ran kii pari khilne ke alaava kallis (26) ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 70 ran kii saajhedaari bhi kii jisase keker ne 140 ran ke lakshya ko do gend shesh rahete paanch wicket par 140 ran banaakar hasil kar liya
 Kallis also featured in bowling, taking two wickets for 21 runs in four overs
 keker ko antim over main jeet ke liye chah ran chahie the or aswin ne yusuf pathan (12) ko pavilion bhej diya lekin devabrata das (chaar gend main naabad 11, do chauke) ne chaukaa jadkar team ko jeet dilaa di
 Earlier, despite the innings of Suresh Raina (44) and captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (34 not out), the Chennai Super Kings team could score 139 runs for five wickets
 pichley paanch maichon main keker kii yah chauthi jeet he jabaki deccan chargers ke khilaaf uskaa ek match barish kii bhent chadh gaya
 The team has now reached second place with 13 points from 10 matches, while Chennai's team is at fourth place with nine points from 10 matches
 gambhir ne shaadaab jakaati or albi morkal par chauke ke saath keker ko prabhavi shuruuaat dilaai lekin ravichandran aswin ne tisare over main brandam maikulam (02) ko pavilion bhej diya

 kallis haalanki dwen braavo kii gend ko drive karne kii koshish main wicket ke peeche dhoni ko kaich dekar pavilion laut gaye

 gambhir ne iske baad manoj tiwari (13) ke saath milakar pari ko aage badhaayaa

 morkal ne haalanki tiwari ko yo mahesh ke haathon kaich kara diya

 isse pehle tas jitkar ballebaaji karne utre chennai kii shuruuaat kharaab rahi or usne paanch over main 32 ran tak hi donon salaami ballebaajon phalf du plasis (03) or mike hasi (18) ke wicket ganvaa die
 Plessis was caught by wicketkeeper Brandon mccullum off paceman Brett Lee in the second over of the innings while Hussey, who was associated with the team, returned to the pavilion to take the run after Australia's West Indies tour ended
 braavo 11 ran ke nijee score par bhaagyashaalee rahe jab unhen aage badhate dekh westeindies ke unke hamawatan aaf spinner naren ne leg said par wide gend phenki lekin maikulam ne stump kaa mauka ganvaa diya
 Bravo, however, could not take advantage of this life and was caught by Abdullah at long on in an attempt to pick up the ball from Kallis
 tippaniyan Kolkata bowlers, meanwhile, began to clamp down on the Chennai batsmen and there were no fours or sixes for 46 balls
